[30;1m111 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m112 | [0m[35mAt the core, a (pydantic) domain model is generated and updated by a bot via[0m
[30;1m113 | [0m[35mpull requests. This model reflects the officially published API specification[0m
[30;1m114 | [0m[35mby Strava and is stored in the module `strava_model.py`. This file should never[0m
[30;1m115 | [0m[35mbe edited manually. Instead, the stravalib bot will suggest changes to the[0m
